     5     39.5 MiB     39.5 MiB           1   def fibs(nmax):
     6                                             """Compute fibonacci number."""
     7     39.5 MiB      0.0 MiB           1       acc = [0, 1]  # Fib(0), Fib(1)
     8                                         
     9     39.5 MiB      0.0 MiB           1       if nmax < 2:
    10                                                 return acc[:nmax + 1]
    11                                         
    12     39.5 MiB      0.0 MiB          30       for n in range(2, nmax + 1):
    13     39.5 MiB      0.0 MiB          29           fib_n_1 = acc[n - 1]
    14     39.5 MiB      0.0 MiB          29           fib_n_2 = acc[n - 2]
    15     39.5 MiB      0.0 MiB          29           fib_n = fib_n_1 + fib_n_2
    16     39.5 MiB      0.0 MiB          29           acc.append(fib_n)
    17                                         
    18     39.5 MiB      0.0 MiB           1       return acc
